--- Sheet: INDEX ---
INDEX | GLOSSARY
S.N | SHEET/REPORT | DATA SOURCE | PURPOSE | S.NO. | TERM | DEFINITION
1 | TEAM MEMBER NAMES & STATIONS | From DVR app(Daily Visit Report) | To collect area coverage details from DVR so management can clearly see which team member handles which area for better planning and monitoring. | 1 | GL | GOOD LUCK PUBLISHERS LTD.
2 | TOUR PROGRAM | Rec'd. from executives through mail or WhatsApp every month.
They fill out information in the company made tempalate. | To record monthly tour schedules received from executives, ensuring all field movement is tracked and properly planned. Also helpful in calculating T.A etc | 2 | VP | VIDYARTHI PRAKASHAN LTD.
3 | BUSINESS & EXPENSE CHART | Combining one year data, including Excel & software files (Supply, Pay, Expense)
 Including:-
 Sale Target, I.P, Gross Supply, Return %, Net Supply, Payment %, Balance, Salary, Salary Expense, TA/DA, Specimen, Salary Expense %, TA/DA Expense %, Specimen %, Total % | To combine one year’s supply, payment, and expense data, giving a complete yearly view of business performance versus expenses. | 3 | CN | CREDIT NOTE- A credit note is a amount a seller (in this case goodluck) issues to reduce or cancel an amount previously billed to a buyer. It is calculated on returns, damaged booksetc.
4 | OLD BALANCE | From Excel files maintained in the office of respective states. | To track pending outstanding amounts using updated Excel files so overdue payments can be followed up and recovered efficiently. | 4 | OPENING | If some party has credit amount of the last years supply.
5 | SUPPLY & PAYMENT FILE | Software & Customer sale with payment report | To maintain a complete yearly financial picture and customer payment reports, supporting accurate accounting and yearly analysis. | 5 | CLOSING | Total amount the party has to pay after deducting all Cn, Extra CN, openings and misc. charges.
6 | SUMMARY CHART YEAR WISE | According to file updated from Software | To prepare annual summary charts from STS (sales tracking system) data, showing year-to-year performance trends for decision-making. | 6 | EXTRA CN | When some party asks for extra discounts on the gross supply and Cash Discounts based on their payments in certain months.
7 | COLLECTION | Software & Customer sale with payment report | To track monthly payment collections from STS reports, helping monitor cash flow and financial planning. | 7 | STR | Strength of the school- Number of students in the school
8 | 2 YEARS CITY WISE SALE | According to file updation from Software | To compile 2-year city-wise supply data from STS, allowing comparison of market performance across cities. | 8 | PRESCRIBED DETAILS | Which books were prescribed to the schools by our executives
9 | 2 YEARS TITLE WISE SUPPLY | Directly from Software(pub) | To review title-wise sales of each executive over two years for performance evaluation and improvement. | 9 | BUSINESS | How much gross business executives generated in the school
10 | TOP 10 SUPPLY TITLES | From title-wise file compilation via software(pub) | To identify top 10 supplied titles from compiled data, helping in stock planning and focusing on high-demand titles. | 10 | TRY TO PRESCRIBE THIS YEAR | Which new books our executives tried to prescribe to the school.
11 | I.P COMPARISON CHART (3 YEARS) | Comparison of 3 years I.P reports rec'd. from executives supply | To compare I.P performance over 3 years using executive data for better trend analysis and forecasting. | 11 | YEAR ON YEAR SALES TREND | Year-on-year sales trend compares sales of a period with the same period in the previous year to show growth or decline.
12 | WORKING DAYS FORMAT | From expenses reports & DVR of executives | To calculate working days from DVR and expense reports, helping measure field efficiency and activity levels. | 12 | SCHOOL WISE SALES TARGET | School-wise sales target means setting specific sales goals for each individual school
13 | PROJECT LIST | From director of the company for next year | To maintain the upcoming year’s project list provided by The Director, ensuring clear planning and execution. | 13 | ENGAGEMENT APPROACH FOR DECLINING SCHOOLS | Engagement approach for declining schools refers to the strategy used to re-engage schools whose sales, participation, or performance have dropped.
14 | DVR SUMMARY | Regular DVR reports, Software & Hard copy | To prepare a combined summary of DVR reports from software and hard copy for effective monitoring of daily activities. | 14 | FOR GROWING SALE WHAT APPROACHES WILL DO | Focus on stronger customer relationships, targeted marketing, expanding product reach, improving service quality, and using data insights to capture new opportunities.
15 | I.P SUMMARY | I.P. check with DVR & Summary prepared in our office | To verify I.P data with DVR and prepare a summary, ensuring accurate performance reporting. | 15 | DVR | Daily Visit Report- It is the name we use for our CRM(Customer Relationship Management) software.
16 | SCHOOL SUMMARY CHART (2 YEARS) | Total of CBSE, ICSE & State board schools from DVR | To analyze CBSE, ICSE, and State Board school data over two years, useful for market strategy and planning. | 16 | ACHIEVED I.P | Gross business achieved by the executive in a year.
17 | JOINT WORKING | DVR data | To capture joint working details from DVR, ensuring coordination and effectiveness of joint field visits.

Joint Working is required in case some executive is not able to convince the party or is getting some issue with the party then he/she asks the manager of the state to go with him/her and help him/her out | 17 | DATES IN RED | DATE OF JOINING OF THE EXECUTIVES INTO OUR ORGANIZATION
18 | WORKSHOP VISIT | We have company made template for the product managers who do the workshop and our office staff gets the workshop request from the field executives. Then we check whether the requested P.M is available on that day or not. It is all done on Google Spreadsheet. | To verify workshop visit details through DVR and emails to track training and engagement activities accurately. | 18 | SALE TARGET | The total sales amount planned or expected to achieve in a specific period (month/quarter/year).
19 | MAP | From Google | To gather map data from Google for geographical clarity and area planning. | 19 | I.P | Individual performance of the executive
20 | SUPPLY | Total material/products supplied to the market without adjusting returns or miscellaneous deductions.
21 | RETURN + MISC. RATIO | Percentage of goods returned + miscellaneous deductions compared to Gross Supply.
Formula: (Return + Misc Amount) ÷ Gross Supply × 100
22 | NET SUPPLY | The actual net business value remaining after deducting all returns and miscellaneous amounts from gross supply.
23 | SALARY | Monthly fixed compensation paid to employees.
24 | TA/DA | Expenses paid to employees for official travel, food, lodging, and daily working expenses.
25 | SPECIMEN EXP. | Specimen expense is the allowed specimen limit given to the executive that he can distribute in the schools based on X% of his sales target.
26 | TOTAL EXP. RATIO | Overall expense percentage including Salary + TA/DA + Specimen.
Formula:  (Total Expenses ÷ Net Business) × 100
27 | SPECIMEN RETURN | Specimen Return means the value of unsold specimen books/material that is returned back by schools, teachers, or field staff.
28 | NET SPECIMEN | Net Specimen means the actual specimen cost after adjusting (subtracting) the specimen returns.
29 | TOTAL AMOUNT | Total Amount means the complete final value after adding all relevant items together (such as sales, expenses, payments, or quantities).
30 | GROSS EXP. % ON I.P | Gross Expense on I.P. means the total expenditure (Salary + TA/DA + Specimen + Other expenses) calculated on the basis of I.P. amount.
31 | NET EXP. % | Net Expense means the final total expenditure after adjusting any deductions such as returns, recoveries, or non-chargeable amounts.
32 | STS | It is software( Spring Time Software). We call it cloudpub.
33 | GROSS | Actual value
34 | NET | Value after discounts

Joint Working Summary.

From Hard Copy / MS Excel:

TADA Bills Expenses Chart.

Tour Program (Hard Copy & Email).

School & Parties List.

Dashboard.

I.P. Comparison (3 Years).

Schools Summary Chart (2 Years).

Workshop Data.



2. Suggested New Reports/Enhancements (Based on our Vision):

A. Sales & Customer Insights

State-wise & Product-wise Performance Dashboard (Live).

School Prescription Trends (current year vs previous year adoption rates).

Sales Return Trend Analysis (state-wise, product-wise, and reasons).

B. Inventory & Forecasting

Demand-Based Stock Forecasting Report (next 3/6/12 months).

Optimal Print Quantity Recommendations (to reduce overstock & shortages).

C. Finance & Collection

Live Collection Target Tracking (vs actual) – with notifications.

Aging Analysis of Receivables (state-wise, customer-wise).

Specimen Budget Utilization Tracker (per person, live).

Cost of Sales & ROI Report (per product & per region).

D. Team & Operations

Salesperson Performance Dashboard (target vs achievement, state-wise).

Workshop Requirement & Performance Tracking (for product managers).

Expense vs Budget Tracking (TADA, Marketing, Specimen) – Live.

Joint Working Effectiveness Report (impact of combined visits).

E. Management/Strategy Level

Profitability by Product Line/Region.

5-Year Trend Analysis (Sales, Profit, ROI).

Market Penetration & Coverage Report (schools covered vs potential).

Real-time ERP/DVR Integration Dashboard (Power BI) – single-window view of all KPIs.

T.A/D.A . BILL PROCEDURE



STEPS



We receive the hardcopy of all the bills and expenses done by the executives.It has all the receipts.

Fuel slips

Hotel slips

Freight

Sales promotions

Bus, train, taxi, auto

Sweets

Mobile bill

Vehicle maintenance

Other/misc.



          We receive it twice a month for dates 1-15 and 16-30.

A summary is created station wise working days based on the DVR data. 

We divide the days on three criterias:

Local visits

Outstation without night stays

Outstation with night stays

All received invoices and receipts are then verified.If there is some mis-information then it is rectified and deducted from the bill.

Then it is signed by the manager and sent to the accounts department.

We have different payment criteria for different stations, different executives and different types of visits.
